pkg/plugins package. The core signature verification system consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. **Manifest Signing & Signature Calculation** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go):\\nThe `Signature` type implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and is responsible for reading plugin manifests from disk and verifying their signatures. The `Calculate` function processes a plugin and returns its signature status. The `ReadPluginManifestFromFS` function reads the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin filesystem, and the `Verify` function checks the cryptographic signature using OpenPGP. The manifest includes plugin ID, version, file hashes, signing organization, and signature type information. The verification process validates that all plugin files match their recorded hashes and checks that the manifest is properly signed.\\n\\n2. **Signature Validation on Load** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go):\\nThe `Validation` type implements the `Validator` interface and is called during the plugin validation pipeline stage. The `ValidateSignature` function checks the signature status of a plugin and determines if it's authorized to load. It handles signature inheritance from parent plugins, checks core plugin exemptions, and enforces signature validation. Different signature statuses (valid, invalid, modified, unsigned) result in different handling - invalid and modified signatures block loading, while unsigned plugins are subject to the allowlist check.\\n\\n3. **Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go):\\nThe `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface and enforces the allowlist of unsigned plugins. The `CanLoadPlugin` function checks if an unsigned plugin is allowed to load by:\\n- Checking if dev mode is enabled (allows all unsigned plugins)\\n- Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` allowlist from the configuration (pkg/plugins/config/config.go)\\n- Rejecting unsigned plugins not in the allowlist by default\\n\\n4. **Key Management** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go):\\nThe static key retriever provides the default PGP public key used to verify plugin signatures. The key is embedded in the code and retrieved by key ID during signature verification.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Loading Pipeline Integration**:\\nThe signature verification is integrated into the plugin loading pipeline:\\n- **Bootstrap Stage** (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go): Calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate()` to determine the signature status when constructing plugins\\n- **Validation Stage** (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go): Calls `ValidateSignature()` to enforce signature policies before plugins are initialized\\n- **Loader** (pkg/plugins/manager/loader/loader.go): Orchestrates the entire pipeline including discovery, bootstrap, validation, and initialization stages\\n\\n6. **Interfaces & Models**:\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface (pkg/plugins/ifaces.go): Defines plugin authorization logic\\n- `SignatureCalculator` interface (pkg/plugins/ifaces.go): Defines signature calculation logic\\n- The `Calculate` function processes a plugin and returns its signature status. The `ReadPluginManifestFromFS` function reads the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin filesystem, and the `Verify` function checks the cryptographic signature using OpenPGP. The manifest includes plugin ID, version, file hashes, signing organization, and signature type information. The verification process validates that all plugin files match their recorded hashes and checks that the manifest is properly signed.\\n\\n2. **Signature Validation on Load** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go):\\nThe `Validation` type implements the `Validator` interface and is called during the plugin validation pipeline stage. Different signature statuses (valid, invalid, modified, unsigned) result in different handling - invalid and modified signatures block loading, while unsigned plugins are subject to the allowlist check.\\n\\n3. **Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement** (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go):\\nThe `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface and enforces the allowlist of unsigned plugins.
